Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers</span></div></td></tr></table></div><div style="text-indent:24.75pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">On January 25, 2022, the board of directors of lululemon athletica inc. appointed Alison Loehnis as a member of the board of directors. Ms. Loehnis is president of Luxury and Fashion at Yoox Net-a-Porter where she is responsible for Net-a-Porter, Mr. Porter and the Outnet businesses. She has held several leadership roles with expanding responsibility since she joined the company in 2007 and has been instrumental in the conception and launch of major initiatives including TheOutnet.com and MrPorter.com. Previously, Ms. Loehnis held positions with LVMH, Hachette Filipacchi and The Walt Disney Company, after starting her career with Saatchi &amp; Saatchi. Ms. Loehnis received a degree in Art History from Brown University. </span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-indent:24.75pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">The board of directors increased the size of the board from ten to eleven members and appointed Ms. Loehnis as a Class III director to fill the newly-created vacancy.  Ms. Loehnis will receive compensation for her service as a director consistent with that of our other non-employee directors. A description of our standard compensation arrangements for non-employee directors is included in our proxy statement filed with the SEC on April 20, 2020. We expect Ms. Loehnis to enter into our standard form indemnification agreement for non-employee directors, the form of which is filed with the SEC as Exhibit 10.16 to our registration statement on Form S-1, dated July 9, 2007.</span></div><div style="text-indent:24.75pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><table <DESCRIPTION>APPOINTMENT OF ALISON LOEHNIS TO BOARD OF DIRECTORS
<TEXT>
<!DOCTYPE html PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/loose.dtd"><html><head>

<title>Document</title></head><body><div id="i4fc68b544ab942549d6fd052e0787087_1"></div><div style="min-height:99pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:right"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Exhibit 99.1</font></div><div style="text-align:right"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><img alt="luluwordmarka.jpg" src="luluwordmarka.jpg" style="height:36px;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:186px"></div></div><div style="margin-top:14pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:115%">Alison Loehnis joins lululemon Board of Directors</font></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Vancouver, British Columbia &#8211; January 27, 2022</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> &#8211; lululemon athletica inc. (NASDAQ&#58;LULU) today announced that Alison Loehnis, President of Luxury and Fashion at Yoox Net-a-Porter, has been appointed to serve on its Board of Directors, effective immediately. </font></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8220;Alison Loehnis is a dynamic leader with a remarkable track record of consistently driving growth through her knowledge of consumer and product trends,&#8221; said Glenn Murphy, Chairman of the Board. &#8220;We look forward to benefiting from Alison&#8217;s valuable insights and expertise as lululemon continues to grow around the world.&#8221;</font></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">At Yoox Net-a-Porter, a global leader in online luxury and fashion, Loehnis is responsible for Net-a-Porter, Mr. Porter and The Outnet businesses. She has held several leadership roles with expanding responsibility since she joined the company in 2007 and has been instrumental in the conception and launch of major initiatives including TheOutnet.com and MrPorter.com. Previously, Loehnis held positions within LVMH, Hachette Filipacchi and The Walt Disney Company, after starting her career with Saatchi &#38; Saatchi.</font></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8220;I have been a loyal lululemon customer for a long time and have always admired their ability to drive product innovation that combines both performance and style. I am excited to join the Board of Directors and support the organization as it continues to expand globally while building connected communities across different platforms,&#8221; said Loehnis. </font></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">A New York native, Loehnis resides in London and graduated from Brown University with a degree in Art History.</font></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">About lululemon athletica inc.</font></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">lululemon athletica inc. (NASDAQ&#58;LULU) is a healthy lifestyle inspired athletic apparel company for yoga, running, training, and most other sweaty pursuits, creating transformational products and experiences which enable people to live a life they love. Setting the bar in technical fabrics and functional designs, lululemon works with yogis and athletes in local communities for continuous research and product feedback. For more information, visit www.lululemon.com.</font></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Contacts</font></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Investors&#58; 	border-bottom: 0px solid black;
}

	white-space: nowrap;
}

}

}

}

	text-align: left;
	white-space: normal;
}

}
